100507, Resistance to change, <div><br></div><div><table style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: Lora, serif; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-size: 16px;"><tbody style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><tr style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><td valign="top" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; width: 800px;"><div class="mainContent" style="margin: 0px 0px 33px; padding: 0px; width: 800px; line-height: 33px;"><div class="blueLink" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(20, 100, 244) !important; border-bottom: none !important;"><span class="smallblogy" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(13, 13, 13); font-size: 18px;"><a href="https://simplicable.com/new/top" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); text-decoration-line: none !important; border-bottom: none !important;">top</a>&nbsp;&nbsp; »&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/management" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); text-decoration-line: none !important; border-bottom: none !important;">management</a>&nbsp;&nbsp; »&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/project-management" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); text-decoration-line: none !important; border-bottom: none !important;">project risk&nbsp;</a>&nbsp; »&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/project-risk-examples" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); text-decoration-line: none !important; border-bottom: none !important;">project risk</a></span></div><br style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><div class="headerReadability" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 65px 0px 0px; line-height: 40px;"><h1 style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; font-family: Roboto, serif; font-size: 36px; font-weight: 400; color: rgb(3, 3, 3);">39 Examples of Project Risk</h1></div><div id="messagebox" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"></div><div class="s101" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0) !important; border-bottom: none !important;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="smallblogy" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(13, 13, 13); font-size: 18px;">posted by&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/johnSpacey" rel="author" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); text-decoration-line: none !important; border-bottom: none !important;">John Spacey</a>, November 29, 2015 updated on February 25, 2017</span></div><div class="readability" id="mainreadable" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px 65px 0px 0px; line-height: 38px;"><span class="blogy" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(13, 13, 13); font-size: 22px;"><br style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img srcset="https://blue.simplicable.com/images/midthumb/project-manager-5-171.jpg 350w, https://blue.simplicable.com/images/thumbnails/project-manager-5-171.jpg 650w, https://blue.simplicable.com/images/header/project-manager-5-171.jpg 790w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 350px, (max-width: 800px) 650px, 790px" src="https://blue.simplicable.com/images/header/project-manager-5-171.jpg" class="headerImg" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: none; width: 790px;"><div class="d001" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; width: 1px; height: 30px; clear: both;"></div><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: 700;">Project risks</span>&nbsp;are uncertainties that exposes a project to potential failure to achieve its goals. Identifying, evaluating and&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/risk-treatment" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">treating</a>&nbsp;risks is an ongoing project management activity that seeks to improve project results by&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/risk-avoidance" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">avoiding</a>,&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/risk-reduction" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">reducing</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/risk-transfer" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">transferring</a>&nbsp;risks. Project risk management also provides stakeholders with visibility and clarifies accountability for&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/risk-acceptance" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">accepted</a>&nbsp;risks. The following are&nbsp;<a href="https://simplicable.com/new/business-risk" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">types of risk</a>commonly encountered by projects.<div class="d001" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; width: 1px; height: 30px; clear: both;"></div><h2 style="margin: 0px 0px 8px; padding: 0px; font-family: Bitter, serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: 400; font-size: 32px;">1.&nbsp;<a id="scope-creep" href="http://simplicable.com/new/scope-creep" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; display: inline; text-decoration-line: none !important; color: rgb(13, 13, 13) !important; border-bottom: none !important;">Scope Creep</a></h2>Scope creep is&nbsp;<a href="http://simplicable.com/new/scope-creep" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">uncontrolled change</a>&nbsp;to a project's scope. For example, urgent projects may be attempted on a&nbsp;<a href="http://simplicable.com/new/best-effort-basis" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">best effort basis</a>&nbsp;that neglects rigorous management of project change.<div class="d001" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; width: 1px; height: 30px; clear: both;"></div><h2 style="margin: 0px 0px 8px; padding: 0px; font-family: Bitter, serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: 400; font-size: 32px;">2.&nbsp;<a id="budget" href="http://simplicable.com/new/budget" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; display: inline; text-decoration-line: none !important; color: rgb(13, 13, 13) !important; border-bottom: none !important;">Budget Risk</a></h2>The risk of&nbsp;<a href="http://simplicable.com/new/budget" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">budget control issues</a>&nbsp;such as cost overruns. Budget estimates are based on forward-looking estimates that typically involve<a href="http://simplicable.com/new/budget" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">some degree of uncertainty</a>.<div class="d001" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; width: 1px; height: 30px; clear: both;"></div><h2 style="margin: 0px 0px 8px; padding: 0px; font-family: Bitter, serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: 400; font-size: 32px;">3.&nbsp;<a id="resistance-to-change" href="http://simplicable.com/new/resistance-to-change" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; display: inline; text-decoration-line: none !important; color: rgb(13, 13, 13) !important; border-bottom: none !important;">Resistance To Change</a></h2><a href="http://simplicable.com/new/resistance-to-change" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">Resistance to change</a>&nbsp;is a common occurrence whereby departments and individuals&nbsp;<a href="http://simplicable.com/new/resistance-to-change" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(205, 0, 0); border-bottom: 4px solid rgb(180, 231, 248); text-decoration-line: none !important;">defend the status quo</a>&nbsp;and actively resist projects or organizational changes.</span></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL
